Will our heroines avoid falling victim to the moon's lunacy, or will they be done in by menstruation instead?

A gentle, cool breeze flew past the somber trees, rustling vibrant green leaves. The moon seemed completely ordinary to any human that looked at it. But for youkai, who were attuned by their nature to the lunar cycle, it was simply all wrong. Chapter End Notes

Welcome to the Touhou 8 fic! This is another fic I'm extremely excited to write. This series is coming along smoothly so far, so I hope everything keeps going well! As always, thanks for sticking with me, and your feedback is appreciated!

Okay guys, I am in a bit of a pinch regarding the plot here. The commonly accepted plot of Touhou 8 is that the fake moon is just making the youkai partners upset, leading them to drag the humans along to investigate. Dialogue ingame seems to support this. However while playing Touhou 8 for research, I found out the good endings actually state the fake moon is either:

a. affecting the youkai's powers (boundary team good ending)
b. causing people, humans and youkai alike, to go insane (!) by looking at it (scarlet and netherworld team good endings)
c. sucking away all the magic in Gensokyo (magic team ending)

Also the real moon seems to be affected afterwards, somehow, in how it affects youkai and other things in Gensokyo. Theres tons of other details too, like Kaguya having an underground hideout previously, the fake moon being made of paper mache somehow (unless its an expression), and Yuyuko casually poisoning Eirin's tea so she could kill her and have her as her nurse. Did real Touhou canonically narrowly avoid a KKHTA-esque scenario here? How is the night imperishable (as referred to by Kaguya, Reimu, and Marisa's dialogue) if the passage of time is a MAJOR GAME MECHANIC???

What exactly is the fandom's consensus on what the fuck was even happening in Touhou 8? Do both the real and fake moons cause lunacy? How long did Eirin even have her spell up before the protagonists had her stop it? Is it based to acknowledge "edgy" parts of the backstory (Mokou's canon 300 year long GMod RP RDM spree) or is that cringe? Some of these plot details will appear later in the fic but I'm mostly just interested in the conversation around these story details. Also, the wiki and most fan content doesn't really do a good job of explaining all these things. Probably because either the English translation patch is hard to understand due to lacking nuance from the original Japanese or something, or that ZUN wrote things imprecisely from the start.

So, go ahead and give your input on these details in the comments. As usual, I'm interested in what you guys have to say!

Chapter End Notes

OKAY continuing off of last chapter's end note, apparently the Touhou 8 omake.txt file, when translated into english, provides all the answers I need for the plot.

First off, the incident was created to protect not Kaguya, but Reisen! Flying in the face of literally all of the ingame dialogue and narrative, including Reisen AND Eirin LITERALLY saying her job is to protect KAGUYA SPECIFICALLY. But whatever, that can be excused because its complex Lunarian politics I'll explain in a bit.

So, Eirin casts the fake moon spell because Reisen gets a telepathic message from the other moon rabbits saying they need her back because the Lunar Capital is expecting a literal war against humanity due to them building a base on the moon. They do this because they could just kill the emissaries sent to get her like with Kaguya but don't want more attention. The spell completely stops travel between Earth and the real moon. I dunno if it's intended to just stop Lunarians from coming to Earth or stop Earthlings (Terrans?) from going to the Moon too.

This puts the timing of the incident into the typical "it's been happening for a little while and Reimu is finally pissed off enough to go solve it" territory of normal Touhou, instead of me thinking Eirin's been doing this for several thousand years to protect Kaguya. That's pretty much all that I was confused about. Funnily enough the wiki doesn't even cover this stuff in the plot section, so you need to actually read the translated omake to figure it out.

Also, Eirin kills people? And not moon rabbits, considering she herself was an emissary sent to retrieve Kaguya, but actual Lunarian humans/demigods/whatever they are like Sagume and the Watatsuki sisters. Not only that, but Kaguya's human family, who were all innocent, were possibly murdered by her after she bribed them with the elixir. And the only thing stopping her from killing even more people is not morality but the fact that there's a better course of action. What the fuck? Where did all this stuff go in the fanon work? We lucked out comparatively by having her get flanderized as a funny milf nurse instead of a complete psychopath murderer.

Completely unrelated tangent here but the omake states that the Lunarians themselves told Reisen that they believe that modern humans are technologically advanced enough to have a slight advantage in a war against them, and that they have directly contacted humans before. Keep in mind this is 2 decade old humans, without all the unmanned vehicles and crazy electronic surveillance technology we have now. What the hell I'm now extremely interested in where this was going. No wonder he wrote a manga and an entire novel about this stuff. I wonder if we will ever see this stuff get expanded upon again past LoLK...

BGM: Maiden's Capriccio ~ Dream Battle

Chapter End Notes

Whoa, 700 hits already! This series keeps getting more and more popular with each entry. This popularity is insane! Thank you all for the attention!

Also, thanks to everyone who gave me info back in Chapter 1 about IN's story! I guess it isn't really as confusing as I thought if you go and actually research translated game material, and hear stuff from others. I can finish this fic with full confidence now!

On spell cards: Theres no real consistent classification for last spells/words beyond what happens in Touhou 8 and the aerial fighters so I took the liberty of making it all up myself! In my headcanon, any spell card in SWR/Soku that's a stronger version of an existing one is a last spell, and any of the super strong, fighting game exclusive 5 card spells can be a last word. This way, we can give last spells/words to characters that weren't in either Touhou 8 or the aerial fighters. Note these rules aren't really solid, because I'm sure the games contradict me somewhere. For example, Yukari Train could be seen as a Last Word but she uses an extremely similar spell in AoCF as a normal spell card, so therefore the rules won't apply. Also, death bombing or getting all spells captured (being on the brink of losing) isn't the only way to cast one, you could also be empowered enough by an urban legend/popularity/whatever natural disaster's happening in Gensokyo that week and be able to cast one.

Also note that this stuff isn't really relevant to this series because these are smut fanfics! 99% of the time Touhou plots are low stakes, so it won't be necessary to up the tension and violence like this before they have sex (its not really needed here either but a porn parody gives me enough irony to write "serious" stuff when needed) in most games. There are a few edge cases in the most popular games (the plot point about the scarlet mist making the humans outside possibly destroy Gensokyo and the Saigyou Ayakashi making people kill themselves are actually real) where the stakes rise. But, most of the time it's just someone shitting on Reimu's doorstep and her going out and beating up little girls to calm down (Eiki Shiki, Byakuren, and Miko LITERALLY didn't do anything wrong at all!). Therefore, we won't need to powerscale spell cards most of the time. Consider this stuff internal material, research I gathered solely so I can make Dragon Ball Z jokes more accurately.

Also, apologies for the wait. This chapter is Very Long and the next few will be too, due to how Stage 4 is structured, and also Imperishable Night in general. After this story is concluded, things should go much more smoothly.

Chapter End Notes

Fun Fact: Despite being a midboss with no dialogue or normal spell cards in Touhou 8, Tewi actually has a full-body portrait visible ingame! This is due to her having one that is used in her Last Word in spell practice mode.

Fun Fact 2: If it were actually possible to make nighttime pass by slower like in the game, it absolutely would cause Kaguya's CS 1.6 client to get booted from the server, if her game or computer didn't crash entirely. This is because this time dilation would theoretically fuck up the time signatures on the packets sent between Kaguya's computer and the game server over the Internet, making it impossible for either side to put them in a comprehensible order and process them into actions (such as moving, chat messages, and shooting) performed by Kaguya's player avatar ingame, especially keeping her client in sync with ~9 other people at once. In addition, it would likely crash either her game client or the computer itself. This is because it would mess with the computer's internal clock. Any and all pieces of code that rely on the assumption that time passes at the normal rate would fail, causing probably a bunch of issues all over the computer. It's similar to the Y2K scare, but physically impossible because Gensokyo isn't real.

Even though the Goldsource engine has packet interpolation (rollback for fgc nerds), Kaguya's client essentially running on different temporal rules would still irreperably fuck up her game's ability to send and recieve data to and from the game server. That's networking for you!

I dunno. The game seems to depict it as "slowing the passage of time of day" (aka what time is shown on the clock) to make night last longer instead of slowing time itself (so no slow-mo). Since it effects clocks, it probably effects a computer's internal clock. I dunno though, just a cool thought.

I'll try to keep working on the series but don't be suprised if I go on hiatuses for a while before this fic is done. Also, I may consider skipping around to the other games before I finish this one, just to conserve my attention span and get as much of this done as I can before my hyperfixation burns out. This chapter is just a real doozy because I have to do Tewi justice as well since she's an important character, but also a midboss on Reisen's stage. Chapter 7: Stage FinalA: Doctor Eirin's Daily Dose

Chapter Summary

Reimu and Yukari finally navigate through Eientei's illusory corridors to confront Gensokyo's newest incident mastermind. A genius alien goddess from the Moon, this lunatic doctor has finally lured the human and youkai into her trap. She won't take down her fake moon unless our heroes pass a rigorous health check up. Including the anal probe. Will our heroes finally put an end to the maddening moon and save all of Gensokyo from falling to insanity, or will Eirin's pills prove too big to swallow?

Thanks doc!

Chapter Notes

See the end of the chapter for notes

A long, long corridor. Is it a lunatic illusion being shown by someone?

To the youkai, this closer moon brought faint, nostalgic memories.

STAGE FinalA: The Orb in the Night Sky, Hiding the Princess

~4 am~

BGM: Voyage 1969

Reimu and Yukari reach the end of the hallway. The floor behind them is littered with dispatched rabbit youkai, dusty pawprints, and clumps of white fur. After a whole hour of exterminating nothing but rabbits, the path of most resistance had led the two to this spot. A single doorway was at the end of the hall, on the left wall, with no other corridors or entrances nearby.

"Yukari, those rabbits fought hard to keep us away from here. Do you think they were protecting this door?" Reimu asks.

"They fought, but not very hard. I agree, though. They were probably defending this door because the mastermind is inside!" Yukari answers.

"Then let's head inside and teach her a lesson!" Reimu says, nodding courageously.

Reimu slides open the wooden door. On the other side is another long hallway, almost pitch black. Reimu looks at Yukari, unsure.

"Yukari, look! It's another really long corridor. Strange, huh?" Reimu remarks.

"It is quite strange, Reimu. I wonder, how does it even fit in the mansion?" Yukari ponders.

"Maybe the mastermind can manipulate time and space? Sakuya does something similar at the Scarlet Devil Mansion." Reimu answers.

"That sounds quite plausible. It would also explain how they were able to tamper with the Moon itself, especially from down here in Gensokyo." Yukari reasons.

The youkai steps through the doorway and gestures for Reimu to follow.

"Are you coming, human? We don't have time to waste." she asks.

Inside the hallway, it truly does seem like the corridor stretches on and on forever. What seems like dim white moonlight pours in through the paper screens. Reimu and Yukari start to fly down the corridor, hopeful that the mastermind will be here somewhere.

"Whoa, Yukari, come here for a second! You have to see this!" she says, shocked.

The two of them were looking at the night sky, full of twinkling stars and cloudy nebulas. Except, there wasn't a tree, a mountain, or a stalk of bamboo to be seen. They couldn't even see the ground at all. In fact, this corridor seemed to be floating through outer space!

"This is amazing. I've never seen space up close before!" Reimu exclaims. "I wish Marisa was here to see this. I just know that she would love it..."

The duo peer out of the window into space for a short while. They can see the moon itself floating close by, as if it were just out of reach. Reimu's eyes followed the stars as if they were danmaku. The nighttime sky glimmered more beautifully than any spell card. She wondered if it was even possible to express the beauty of the vast, endless beyond within a spell card.

The uncharted expanse brought back nostalgic memories from deep within Yukari's mind. She had explored this void once. It was one of many worlds she had crossed the boundaries over into. It wasn't her original idea, but she always thought that space held more wonders and possibilities than even Gensokyo. Those days were the ones she cherished the most out of her entire long life. They had to have been... how long ago? It really didn't matter. Not within the grand scheme of things. Within her memories, those days were just one tiny boundary away. "Thank you, Eirin! Oh, my friends, they're all going to be safe! My shrine will be alright. Gensokyo will finally turn back to normal. Maybe I'll even get some more visitors to come and donate on the evening of the festival! Thank you! I promise we'll do whatever we can to stop the humans outside from invading your planet."

Eirin hesitantly hugs the elated miko back.

"Shrine maiden, I am truly sorry for the trouble my rogue scheming almost caused. From now on, I vow to stop putting myself atop a pedestal. I'll stand side by side with you all, human, youkai, and Lunarian. I'll make myself useful to the inhabitants of this land. Surely my vast knowledge of medicine would be useful."

Reimu nods up at her, accepting the apology.

"That would be great, Eirin. I'm sure there is a way for you to help us out. There is room for everyone here in Gensokyo, as long as you respect our society's balance."

Yukari looks on at the tearful episode with a small, wry smile. Yes, this wise Lunarian would be a valuable asset to her. And perhaps someday, after they can properly make amends, a good friend. Benefits or not.

Another thought crosses Yukari's mind. She looks around the surface of the moon. Not a single head of long brunette hair could be seen anywhere. Neither could she spot a single impossible request.

"Wait a second. Where did she go?" Yukari asks.

"Who?" asks Reimu in response.

"The other immortal. The princess."

Chapter End Notes

Whew, so that was one hell of a chapter. What a way to end such a pivotal, amazing game in my, uh, sex porn fanfic. We are at over 2600 hits and 30 kudos, so as usual I thank you all for the overwhelming support. I hope you all enjoyed this installment, and I'll see you all in the PoFV fic when I get back to it! Looking back I realized that this fic is now as long as an actual novel somehow, so I definitely need to take a break before coming back. The rest of the games definitely won't be this long, nor this plot-driven for the most part, so thankfully this will not happen again.

*gmod flatline noise*

Fun fact: Mokou does actually seem to die and resurrect instantly in the extra stage. Apparently some manga or artbook somewhere says that Mokou and the other immortals resurrect after a day, but she does so after you beat every single spell card in the real game. It also kind of suffers from the inconsistency on whether or not danmaku is actually lethal, as she still "dies" from the player's attack. It's stated to be a nonlethal method of conflict resolution focused on bullet hell stuff instead of lethality, but Sakuya literally throws knives at people, multiple characters actually attack with real sword blades in the fighters, there's a teenager carrying a real gun, and even the person who enforces it runs people over with trains (later packed with real chemical explosives). Letting them just murder eachother graphically then come back to life is just cooler in my opinion, so I just assumed they could come back alive instantly and let them go at it. Also, apologies if it grosses you out! ZUN himself writes about people hanging themselves and getting decapitated in Dolls in Pseudo Paradise, so you can't judge me though.

The part with them floating in space is my own tribute to doujins where the immortals live until the end of the universe. I always love reading them, and they always tear me apart emotionally. Though, my take on it is decidedly less religious and much more science fictioney, lewd, apathetic, and tragic. I hope it doesn't upset you all too much with how bleak it is.

Anyways I have no idea if Snake x Otacon was ever genuinely huge in yaoi circles but I rolled with it because I saw that yaoi twitter poll thing and got inspired. I don't know a single thing about Naruto (the most obvious choice) but I instantly came up with like 5 MGS jokes I could do so it was well worth the cringe. Also, I have no idea how Mokou even plays video games, being a hobo, but I made her do so because it's funny.

Also, special thanks to Seelenwanderer for actually suggesting the Morrowind joke to me! I feel like I should probably make a separate fanfic about my headcanons for what outside world interests the Touhou characters have, because this is getting kinda ridiculous, very fast.

As a bonus, see if you can recognize all the cameos I put in at the end!
